[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer-driven test of the Shadowsocks JSON parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`json_fuzz`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m triggered an [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer-detected heap-buffer-overflow in the function `json_parse_ex` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39msrc/shadowsocks/src/json.[0m[1;92mc:327[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. During parsing of a [0m[1;36m13[0m[39m-byte input, the code [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperforms a one-byte read just past the end of an allocated buffer, leading to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory corruption and program abort.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIssue Details  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer harness invokes `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`, which in turn calls [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`json_parse` and `json_parse_ex` to process arbitrary input.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- AddressSanitizer reports a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read at address [0m[1;36m0x5020000000bd[0m[39m, which is [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexactly one byte beyond a [0m[1;36m13[0m[39m-byte heap allocation [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x5020000000b0[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x5020000000bd[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow is classified as “heap-buffer-overflow” [0m[1;39m([0m[39mscariness [0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`json_parse_ex` at line [0m[1;36m327[0m[39m of json.c.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mVulnerability Type  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Heap-based buffer overflow: the parser reads beyond the allocated buffer bounds.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mKey Observations  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The offending read occurs in `json_parse_ex`, indicating a missing or incorrect [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundary check when consuming input.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The backtrace shows the flow: `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` → `json_parse` → [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`json_parse_ex`.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ASan shadow-memory output confirms that the byte being accessed lies in the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mredzone immediately after the allocated region.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow consistently reproduces under interactive libFuzzer settings with a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtimeout of 25s and [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m test runs.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPoints of Investigation  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The implementation of `json_parse_ex` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/shadowsocks/src/json.c around line [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m327[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for buffer-length checks.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The higher-level `json_parse` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39msame source file, line [0m[1;36m958[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to verify how[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit invokes `json_parse_ex` and manages input lengths.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Any helper functions or loops in json.c that scan or copy data from the input [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer and may lack proper boundary validation.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The initialization and allocation logic for the input buffer passed to the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser, to confirm its size and lifetime semantics.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNote  [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`json_fuzz.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m serves only as an entry point and is not the [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow occurs on a `READ of size [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` at an address immediately past a [0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstring.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The check `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` precedes four successive `*++state.ptr`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations, but evidently fails to prevent reading one byte beyond the buffer.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The patch changes the condition from `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` to `end - state.ptr < [0m [2m                [0m
